#Development File
#Doing development by itself here for easier organization and editing
#
#
#1124 - +3
#
#1166 - Start of High Middle Age +4
#
#1204 - High Middle Age +5
#
#1241 - Start of Late Middle Age +4
#
#1310 - Late Middle Age +6
#
#Development only changes the de_jure territory. So no need to add dates for titles that no longer exist ie Lotharingia which is split into Upper/Lower Lorraine. Numbers are pretty arbitrary and I'm not going to look up whether the Duchy of Blois was more 'developed' than the Duchy of Valois so their 1100 number will be the same just like it is in 1000.
#
#   - Areas will lose development where needed. For example Constantinople during 1204 or parts of the Middle East due to Mongol Conquests such as Baghdad or Khwarazm.
#	- Individual counties/duchies may be higher than the Kingdoms overall setting. Generally speaking this means major cities and capitals
#

##Other File - Empire Titles. Overall lowered as default numbers Paradox had for 1100 were too high. All empire titles have to be at the top of the file
